力着，「淸明時節」如果好，這是大家的力量，反之，那是導演應當負責的。英雄末路　　大上海映

1936.12.22

Huang Shao-xiong Arrives in Taiyuan to Confer with Yan, Thoroughly Discussing the Response to the Shaanxi Incident, Zhao, Xu, and Others Participate in the Discussions, Wan Fulin Once Sent Personnel to Visit Yan 1

(Taiyuan) Huang Shao-xiong arrived in Taiyuan this afternoon by Zhengtai train. Zhao, Xu, Yang, and various military and political leaders all went to the station to welcome him. He is staying at the Shanxi Grand Hotel. Yan had gone to the hotel to greet him in advance. They conferred with Huang and others on the Shaanxi Incident for over an hour. Afterward, they rode together to the Suiyuan Headquarters for a banquet hosted by Yan. During the banquet, they conducted detailed discussions with Zhao, Xu, and others. (21st Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) Wan Fulin, considering the severity of the situation in Shaanxi and its significant impact on the nation and the people, sent a telegram to the central government expressing his stance. Yesterday, he sent a representative, Wu Songlin, to Taiyuan to visit Yan. After visiting Yan this morning, Wu returned to Baoding tonight to report back. (21st Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) This morning, during the memorial week, Yan expressed his views on the Shaanxi Incident, saying that this incident is not only a great misfortune for the nation and the people from below but also holds unlimited hidden worries for the future. We should bravely advance and save this critical situation. The primary task is to first ask Chiang to return to Nanjing. I will continue to work day and night towards this goal. Furthermore, Shanxi and Suiyuan are at the forefront of national defense. Only by working together with one heart and being determined to make the greatest sacrifices can we defend our territory and resist the war. (21st Dispatch)

Various Circles in Hankou and Xiamen Held Meetings Yesterday to Condemn the Rebellion, Condemnatory Telegrams from All Quarters Arrived Like Snowflakes 2

(Hankou) At 2:00 PM on the 21st, various circles in Hankou held a meeting at the city party headquarters to condemn the rebellion. The atmosphere at the meeting was extremely solemn. More than 500 representatives from various agencies and organizations attended. After performing the rituals, Chen Panling, a special commissioner from the city party headquarters, presided over the meeting and reported the significance of the meeting. Subsequently, He Chengjun, representing Chen Guangzu, the mayor of Hankou, Wu Guozhen, and others, delivered speeches. The following resolutions were passed: (1) A nationwide telegram to condemn the rebellion and quell the chaos; (2) A telegram to Commander-in-Chief He, urging him to quickly quell the chaos and escort Chairman Chiang back to Nanjing; (3) A telegram to comfort Chairman Chiang; (4) Urging the city's escort committee representative delegation to go north immediately. Finally, the entire assembly stood in solemn oath before dispersing. (21st Central News Agency)

(Xiamen) Various circles in Fujian unanimously support condemning the rebellion and rescuing Chiang: (1) Various circles in Xiamen held a meeting on the 21st to support the central government's condemnation of the rebellion and took an oath; (2) Quanzhou held a meeting on the 20th of all circles in Jinjiang to rescue Chairman Chiang and return him to Nanjing to preside over the government; (3) Zhangzhou held a meeting on the 20th of all circles to quell the difficulties and save the country. Tong'an, Nan'an, Zhangpu, and Longyan each held meetings and issued telegrams. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Since Zhang's rebellion, condemnatory telegrams from all quarters have arrived like snowflakes. Among those received by the National Government on the 21st were from Xue Yue, officers and soldiers of the Hubei Provincial Security Corps, civilian organizations in Suiyuan Province, the Chongqing Municipal Mountain Goods and Medicinal Materials Trade Association, all students of Anhui University, and many other places. (21st Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) Zhang Zhengzhai, a staff officer of the 165th Division stationed in Minxian, Zhang Jueseng, Zhang Gancheng, and Lu Min, students of the Military Academy's Advanced Education Class, recently received a joint telegram from their division commander Lu Dachang and deputy division commander Jiang Hancheng and others, vowing to support the central government and asking to be allowed to fight the rebels. The original telegram stated: (Omitted). "We have received your telegram. Zhang's rebellion against the party and harm to the country, occupying Xi'an, and holding the commander-in-chief hostage, making presumptuous claims, such disloyal, rebellious, ungrateful, and unrighteous wolfish ambition is intolerable to both heaven and earth, and despised by China and foreign countries. The central government, for the sake of rectifying the steel discipline and laying the foundation of the country, can only quickly launch a campaign to destroy the rebels. Our division belongs to the military and should sincerely support the central government, be ready for battle, and annihilate this rebellion. However, due to the remote location and blocked transportation, we ask to request instructions from the central government nearby so that we can follow them. Lu Dachang, Jiang Hancheng, Liang Yingkui, Wang Chengyi, and the entire division of officers and soldiers kowtow." (21st Central News Agency)

All Circles Take an Oath to Be Loyal to the Party and the Country 3

(Nanjing) This morning, all circles in Nanjing took an oath to be loyal to the party and the country and immediately formed a national salvation and crisis response corps to rescue Chairman Chiang from danger and, in the name of the general assembly, sent a telegram to the whole country to support the central government, quickly punish Zhang's rebellion, and comfort the frontline soldiers fighting the enemy in Suiyuan. It was also decided to prohibit dancing and musical entertainment during the leader's crisis. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) During the memorial week on the 21st, the Nanjing Municipal Government, led by Mayor Ma Chaojun, took an oath to be loyal to the party and the country, implement the Three Principles of the People, support Chairman Chiang, and ensure that the leader can safely exercise his powers, continue to lead the country, complete the defense against foreign aggression, save the country, and revitalize the nation. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) During the memorial week held by the Ministry of Interior on the morning of the 21st, all 300+ employees took an oath to be loyal to the party and the country and support Chairman Chiang, led by Tao Luqian, who read the oath. (21st Central News Agency)

(Guangzhou) The Guangzhou City Party Headquarters held a meeting after the joint memorial week of all circles on the 21st and decided to: (1) Form a delegation of all circles in Guangdong to welcome the leader back to Nanjing; (2) Take an oath to be loyal to the party and the country and support Chairman Chiang. (Central News Agency)

Dong Zhao's Division's Advance Team Has Reached Chishui, Feng Qinzaib's Troops Advance Westward Side by Side, Rebellious Troops in Weinan Increase Preparations for Battle 4

Huayin: Dong Zhao, leading his troops, recovered Huazhou City on the 20th, completely disarming two battalions of rebel troops, and seizing a large amount of weapons, ammunition, and supplies. Currently, the advance team of the National Army has reached Chishui, and Feng Qinzaib's troops are advancing westward side by side with the Central Army. (21st Central News Agency)

(Zhengzhou) The Zhengzhou-Shaanxi telegraph has been restored. Rumors that Xu Haidong has arrived in Xi'an have been verified by all parties as inaccurate. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Wang Luyi telegraphed Nanjing from Tongguan, stating that he arrived in Tongguan on the 19th. Chief Director Xu Tingyao, Army Commander Fan Songfu, and Guo Yangfen, the deputy commander of Feng Qinzaib's troops, met with the President and are currently discussing the matter. There are four things to report: 1. Zhang visits the President every day, bowing respectfully and standing for a long time, saying that from the President's diary, he knows that the President has no other intentions towards him, expressing remorse. The President is also slightly lenient towards him. 2. Personnel in southeast Xi'an have been arrested and robbed very cruelly. 3. Bombs have been dropped in Weinan, Huayin, Sanyuan, and other places. The Weinan railway station and the rebel army's ammunition depot have been destroyed. 4. The rebel troops stationed in Tianshi Town threaten the Xi'an-Tongguan transportation and will destroy it. The President is healthy. Wang Luyi. (21st Dispatch)

(Luoyang) Military news: (1) Weinan has added one rebel special task force and one artillery regiment and has transported a large amount of lead wire and various equipment and materials, making urgent preparations for battle; (2) Aerial reconnaissance reports that a unit of troops has crossed the river south from Chaoyi and has a pontoon bridge at Qinglongzhen and is building a bridge near Chishui; (3) According to reports, Miao Zhengliu telegraphed to Chang Enduo, commander of the rebel 111th Division, Shen Ke, commander of the 106th Division, and Zhao Yi, commander of the 120th Division, that he had received an order from the rebel Zhang, stating that this side is eagerly awaiting troops, and they should quickly equip their main forces lightly and rush forward day and night, reporting their arrival at each location after encamping. (11th Central News Agency)

Shao Yuan Chong's Reason for Entering Shaanxi 5

(Nanjing) Li Hongwen, the representative of Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Taiyuan, told reporters on the 21st that the reports about the inside story of Mr. Shao Yuan Chong's entry into Shaanxi were not detailed. I fully understand the reason why Shao entered Shaanxi. Two days before Shao went to Shaanxi, I met with Mr. Chen Zifeng at his residence to jointly discuss a plan to recruit and pacify several informal troops in Suiyuan who were under the coercion of bandits. These troops had long had the intention of surrendering, but because no one could speak on their behalf, they had no choice but to wave the flag for other bandits. Mr. Shao and I understood the intentions of these people, and there were many people who could be persuaded, so it was decided that Mr. Shao would personally go to Shaanxi to discuss the matter with Chairman Chiang in a serious manner, so as to achieve twice the result with half the effort. After Mr. Shao entered Shaanxi, he met with Chairman Chiang several times about this matter, and Chairman Chiang agreed very much and had already implemented it according to Mr. Shao's plan. The detailed process and the names of the recruited troops are confidential and cannot be disclosed. On the 10th of this month, Mr. Shao planned to return south immediately after completing his mission, because before Mr. Shao flew to Shaanxi, he had to return to Nanjing from the southwest to deal with other important matters in Nanjing. However, because Chairman Chiang repeatedly persuaded him to stay, he could not make the trip. Unexpectedly, the Shaanxi Incident broke out suddenly on the 12th, and Mr. Shao suddenly encountered the rebellion and died. However, I have received news from the front that the troops that Mr. Shao had previously planned to recruit have all surrendered one after another. The current improvement of the Suiyuan situation is greatly related to this. However, Mr. Shao has already achieved success and died. It is so painful! (21st Central News Agency)

Long Yun Telegraphed Commander-in-Chief He to Send a Representative to Nanjing 6

Kunming: Long Yun received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief He (dated the 16th), stating that he was ordered to relieve the crisis and save the country, bearing heavy responsibilities, and had many things to ask for advice. He hoped that Long could take the time to go to Nanjing for a trip to discuss the best plan, but if he was too busy to leave, he asked him to send a representative to come. Long replied to He on the 18th, stating that due to the initial outbreak of the incident, in order to stabilize the hearts of the people, he would not go to Nanjing for the time being and had entrusted Huang Shijun to fly to Nanjing by plane and would send Gao Yinhuai to pay a visit and learn everything. If Long was still needed to come after Huang and Gao reported back, he would pack his bags and set off. (20th Central News Agency)

Ma Chaojun Telegraphed Gui Yongqing 7

(Nanjing) Ma Chaojun telegraphed to Tongguan on the 21st, sending greetings to Gui Yongqing, the commander of the Training Corps: "The rebellious bandits in Xi'an are harming the country. You, my brother, are leading your troops on a swift expedition to punish them. I am pleased to hear that wherever your banners go, Huaxian has already been recovered. I hope that you will uphold the spirit of Dongjiang in punishing the rebellion and write a great continuation of quelling the chaos in the northwest. Advance day and night and besiege the rebels immediately, so that the chief culprit will be captured and the President will be rescued from danger. The fate of the country depends on this. I and the strong men of the capital have long been trained by the President, and we are deeply shocked and angered by this incident. We all have the determination to kill the bandits and vow to be your backing. I send a special telegram to congratulate you." (Telegram on the 21st)

Guangzhou Joint Memorial Week Reports on the Shaanxi Incident 8

(Hong Kong) During the joint memorial week on the 21st, Yu Hanmou reported that Zhang Xueliang forcibly detained the President at a time when the national unification and bandit suppression had been victorious. No matter how he defended himself, he would eventually be abandoned by the people of the country. Therefore, after receiving the news, I and Chairman Huang were the first to express our opposition. However, based on observation at this time, three conclusions can be drawn: (1) Unifying against foreign aggression is the unanimous demand of the whole country; (2) Chiang is the center of unifying against foreign aggression and the leader believed in by the people; (3) Anyone who violates the demands of the people and hinders the leader will be abandoned by the people. We only know that the Three Principles of the People are the only doctrine to save China and that we must concentrate the strength of the whole country under the overall national policy and central leadership to complete the great cause of national revitalization. The current important work in this province is to protect the locality, maintain finance, prevent traitors, and protect foreigners. (11th Dispatch)

(Guangzhou) People here are eagerly awaiting the development of the overall situation in Xi'an. Officials held a meeting today and swore to be loyal to the central government in any situation. Today, Yu Hanmou issued a declaration stating that Guangdong Province is willing to do its best to support the central government and is determined to protect Guangzhou at all costs. He also said that the current work in Guangdong Province is nothing more than the following four points: (1) Protect the security of the local area; (2) Maintain the local finance; (3) Strictly prevent reactionaries; (4) Protect foreigners. It is reported that Zhang Yingmin, the chief of staff of Guangxi Province, has recently suspended his trip to the north and has returned to Guilin to discuss the political situation with other leaders of Guangxi Province. (21st Reuters)

Song Ziwen Flies to Nanjing from Xi'an, It is Reported That This Trip Is to Welcome Madam Chiang to Shaanxi 9

(Nanjing) Song Ziwen flew from Nanjing to Luoyang on the afternoon of the 19th, staying overnight due to the clouds. He flew to Shaanxi at 8:00 AM on the morning of the 20th. When he landed in Xi'an, the rebel Zhang Xueliang and the rebel Yang Hucheng rushed to the airport to greet him. Then he went to the Xi'an Guest House to rest and talked briefly. Zhang accompanied him to meet Chairman Chiang. After completing his business, Song took the original plane back to Nanjing from Xi'an at 12:00 PM on the 21st, arriving at 4:25 PM. He Yingqin, Minister of Military and Political Affairs, Zou Lin, Vice Minister of Finance, Qin Fen, Secretary of the Economic Commission, Ma Chaojun, Mayor, Liu Ruiheng, Director of the Health Administration, and others all went to the airport to meet him. Song got off the plane and went to Kong's residence at Gaoloumen to meet Madam Chiang Song Meiling, Kong Xiangxi, Acting President of the Executive Yuan, and Madam Kong to report on the trip. Then he met with Minister He and others to talk. Song stayed in Xi'an for 24 hours. His accompanying secretaries Chen Kangqi and Chen Fengyi returned together. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Two flight instructors who were injured in Xi'an on the 12th arrived in Nanjing at 3:50 PM on the afternoon of the 21st by Ford plane. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Song Ziwen, due to personal relations, accompanied by his staff Chen Kangqi and Chen Fengyi, flew from Nanjing to Xi'an on the 19th to visit Chairman Chiang. However, due to snow when passing through Luoyang, he landed and changed to fly west from Luoyang at 8:00 AM on the morning of the 20th, arriving outside Xi'an City at 10:00 AM. Zhang Xueliang and others all went to greet him and accompanied Mr. Song by car into the city to meet Chairman Chiang to pay his respects. Mr. Song has now completed his business and departed from Xi'an by plane on the afternoon of the 21st at 12:30 PM, arriving in Nanjing at 4:30 PM. He Yingqin, Chen Bulei, Liu Ruiheng, Qin Fen, Zou Lin, Ma Chaojun, and more than 20 other people went to Minggugong Airport to welcome him. After Mr. Song got off the plane, he shook hands with the welcoming staff to thank them and then drove to Kong's residence to meet Acting President Kong and Madam Chiang to talk. It is reported that Mr. Song returned to Nanjing to welcome Madam Chiang to Shaanxi. (21st Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) Song Ziwen flew to Nanjing from Xi'an this afternoon. While in Xi'an, Song met with both Chairman Chiang and Zhang Xueliang. Senior officials here all went to the airport at 2:00 PM this afternoon to welcome him. However, the plane carrying Mr. Song did not arrive in Nanjing until 3:30 PM. After Mr. Zhu got off the plane, he went to Kong Xiangxi's residence to report to Madam Chiang on his meeting with Chairman Chiang and Zhang Xueliang. (21st Reuters)

Kawagoe Visits Zhang to Express Concern About the Shaanxi Incident, Japanese Observers Believe a Compromise in the Shaanxi Incident Is Unlikely, British and American Ambassadors Also Visit Zhang and Xu to Inquire About News 10

(Nanjing) Japanese Ambassador Kawagoe, who went to Shanghai on the 5th, has been there for half a month. Now, out of concern for Chairman Chiang's situation in Shaanxi, he came to Nanjing the day before yesterday. At 4:30 PM on the 21st, he went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs with his secretary Shimizu to meet Foreign Minister Zhang to express his concern and talk about Sino-Japanese incidents. (21st Dispatch)

Kong Xiangxi, Niu Yongjian, Zhang Ji, Wang Zhengting, Deng Jiayan, Li Wenfan, Jing Hengyi, Wang Boqun, Ma Chaojun, Liu Jiwen, Lin Yunshan, Chen Shaokuan, Wang Yongbin, Chen Shuren, Chen Xunyong, Chen Qicai, Lv Chao, Wei Huai and others, as well as more than 600 officials from the National Government and various departments and ministries, attended. Chairman Lin led the ceremony and gave an impromptu speech on "The Great Significance of the Central Government's Clear Order to Punish the Rebels." The ceremony concluded at 10:30 a.m. (21st Central Telegram)

(Nanjing) Chairman Lin reported at the National Government Memorial Week on the morning of the 21st, entitled "The Greatest Significance of the Central Government's Clear Order to Punish the Rebels." The original speech was as follows: "The Xi'an Incident occurred last Saturday and today is the ninth day. You can all see the course of events in the newspapers, so there is no need for me to report them again. What I want to report to you today is why the Central Government resolutely and decisively issued a clear order to punish the rebels. Speaking of this reason, it is actually very clear. First, from the perspective of our Party, the rebel Zhang Xueliang was originally a Party member. He should have obeyed Party discipline and Party principles. His actions should have been loyal to the Party and loyal to the ideology. The Central Government ordered him to take charge of the work of suppressing the bandits. He should have, under the command of the Central Government, supervised and led his troops to completely wipe out the remaining bandits in the Northwest. Unexpectedly, over the years, he wasted a lot of the country's military expenses and consumed a lot of precious time. As a result, he was raising bandits and aggrandizing himself. Recently, he dared to violate the major policies repeatedly decided by the Central Government, colluding with bandits, and kidnapping the Commander-in-Chief, creating the unprecedented Xi'an Incident. Such betrayal of the Three People's Principles and harm to the Chinese Kuomintang is a crime that cannot be tolerated. In order to maintain Party principles and Party discipline, the Central Government has no room for leniency towards such traitors. This is the first significance of the Central Government's decision to clearly order the punishment of the rebels. Second, from the perspective of the country, the reason why a country can be established, maintain national order, and maintain national unity lies entirely in the two words: 'principle' and 'discipline'. If a country has principles and discipline, the country can survive and maintain national security. If a country has no principles and discipline, the country will perish and will not be able to maintain all the order of national society. Therefore, principles and discipline are necessary conditions for the survival of a country. This rebel Zhang Xueliang committed treason and rebellion in Xi'an, kidnapping the Commander-in-Chief, and destroying the country's principles and discipline completely. In order to rectify the principles and discipline of the country, the Central Government has no room for turning back in punishing the rebel Zhang Xueliang. This is the second significance of the Central Government's decision to clearly order the punishment of the rebels. Third, from the perspective of the nation, every nation that can survive in the world has a basis for survival. Our Chinese nation has our Chinese nation's history, our Chinese nation's environment, and therefore our Chinese nation has our Chinese nation's basis for survival. In the current situation, our Chinese nation's basis for survival, simply put, is to clear the banditry at home and resist the powerful abroad. On the one hand, we must eliminate the remaining bandits in the country, and on the other hand, we must resist foreign aggression. These two tasks should be considered together. We must not focus on one and lose sight of the other, and we must not invite wolves to repel tigers. We must seek national self-reliance and national rejuvenation on this basis. Only then can our Chinese nation achieve the goal of true freedom and equality. This time, the rebel Zhang Xueliang, under the guise of resisting insults, colluded with the remaining bandits and spread heresies. If his rebellious plot succeeds, it would be a case of the wolves advancing before the tigers are repelled, harming the survival of the Chinese nation to the extreme. In order to safeguard the survival of the entire nation, the Central Government should severely punish the rebel Zhang Xueliang and have no room for tolerance. This is the third significance of the Central Government's decision to clearly order the punishment of the rebels. Fourth, from the perspective of morality, our late Premier Sun Yat-Sen vigorously advocated promoting our Chinese inherent morality. Among the inherent virtues of China, the four words of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and righteousness occupy the most important position. This time, the rebel Zhang Xueliang betrayed the Party and the country, committing treason and rebellion. He is disloyal. His father's revenge has not been avenged and the lost land has not been recovered. Instead, he took advantage of the normal and urgent time of the Sui War to turn to rebellion, creating an opportunity for the enemy to invade. He is unfilial. Because of a single thought, he made tens of thousands of children of Northern Shaanxi his personal sacrifices. He is unbenevolent. He is ungrateful to his superiors, repaying kindness with hatred. He is unrighteous. The people of the country are deeply indignant at this traitor who is disloyal, unfilial, unbenevolent, and unrighteous. The Central Government, based on the principle that all Chinese people can kill such a person, launched a major crusade. This is the fourth significance of the Central Government's order to punish the rebels this time. The above is my explanation today of the great significance of this decision to clearly order the punishment of the rebels. In short, the most important thing for the Party is ideology, the most important thing for the country is principles and discipline, the most important thing for the nation is survival, and the most important thing for morality is loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and righteousness. The perverse actions of the rebel Zhang Xueliang this time are a betrayal of the Party's ideology, a destruction of the country's principles and discipline, a harm to the nation's survival, and a lack of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and righteousness. They are resented by the world and abandoned by all. Not only should the Central Government issue a clear order to punish him, but all Chinese people should beat the drums and attack him, and should rise up to punish him, so that justice can be extended, the source of chaos can be eliminated, and traitors and rebellious sons will be frightened and lose their souls, so that there will be no second Zhang Xueliang. This is the hope for the future of the country and the nation. (21st Central News Agency Telegram)

Tianjin People's Hearts Gradually Stabilize; Market Becomes More Stable Day by Day 25

(Tianjin) The hearts of the people of Tianjin are gradually stabilizing, and they are convinced that Chiang is safe and will be out of danger soon, and that the Shaanxi Incident can be resolved. Ministry of Railways Signs a 40 Million Loan Contract with German Merchants to Construct the Hunan-Guizhou Railway and Repair the Yellow River Bridge 26

(Nanjing) In order to raise funds for the construction of the Hunan-Guizhou Railway and the repair of the Pinghan Yellow River Railway Bridge, the Ministry of Railways specially negotiated with German merchants Otto Wolff and others on the method of borrowing materials. Negotiations began in the spring and a preliminary contract was signed. After consultations with various parties, the purchase contract was finally agreed upon recently and formally signed after being approved by the government. The total amount of the material loan is 40 million yuan, with an annual interest rate of 6%. Of this amount, 30 million yuan will be used for the construction of the Hunan-Guizhou Railway, and the remaining 10 million yuan will be used for the repair of the Pinghan Yellow River Railway Bridge. The repayment period is ten years for the 30 million yuan for the Hunan-Guizhou Railway and twelve years for the 10 million yuan for the Pinghan Railway. The material loan will be secured by the future property and income of the railway, and the German side will entrust the Bank of China as the trustee, with detailed provisions regarding the exercise of the mortgage rights. The Bank of China will come forward to investigate. The Hunan-Guizhou Railway starts from Zhuzhou in Hunan to Guiyang in Guizhou, with a total length of 1,002 kilometers, and is the backbone of transportation in the Southwest. Construction has already begun and is expected to be completed in three years, which will be of great benefit to the progress of the national railway construction plan. (21st Central News Agency Telegram)

(Berlin) The Ministry of Railways of the Chinese National Government has signed a contract with the German companies Ferrostaal, Fried. Krupp Stahl Union Export GmbH, and Wolff and others, stipulating that the above-mentioned companies will supply railway materials on credit up to a limit of 40 million yuan. Of this amount, 30 million yuan will be used to build and equip a new railway line from Zhuzhou, Hunan to Guiyang, Guizhou, and the remaining 10 million yuan will be used to rebuild the Yellow River Railway Bridge on the Pinghan Railway. The credit granted by German manufacturers will be repaid in twelve years (referring to the 30 million yuan for the construction of the railway) and ten years (referring to the 10 million yuan for the reconstruction of the Yellow River Railway Bridge), with an annual interest rate of 3%. The new railway line is an extension westward of the Nanping (from Nanchang to Pingxiang Railway), and that railway will be used as collateral for the 30 million yuan credit. This contract is the result of nearly a year of continued consultations following the preliminary contract established by both parties on January 22 of this year. (21st National Telegram)

The council has specially divided Daxing, Wanping, Tongxian, Changping and other four counties into one administrative region, with the Wanping county magistrate concurrently serving as the administrative commissioner. Jinghai, Wuqing, Ninghe and other four counties in Tianjin were divided into one administrative region, with the Tianjin county magistrate concurrently serving as the administrative commissioner. As for the three items of bandit suppression, diplomacy and transportation, which are related to the Beiping Municipality in Wanping county and the jurisdiction, and are related to the Tianjin Municipality in Tianjin county and the jurisdiction, the commissioner will be directly under the jurisdiction and command of the mayor of Beiping and Tianjin in order to be able to follow instructions. The council has issued orders to the Hebei-Beiping-Tianjin provincial and municipal governments on the 21st to comply with the implementation. (21st Central News Agency Telegram)

Current Events Commentary

Judiciary Authorities Accuse the Department of Justice 37

— By Zhong

It is reported that Zhang Xueliang, in addition to betraying the party and the nation, also condoned soldiers and bandits, resulting in murder and arson. In the Xi'an area, the number of people killed is not small. To rectify the legal system, the Ministry of Judicial Administration has ordered the Prosecutor's Office of the Supreme Court to instruct its subordinates to conduct a thorough investigation. After receiving the order, the Prosecutor's Office has notified all its subordinates to comply and has submitted a report for review. It is expected that those who disturb the people will be brought to justice, and the law will be sufficient to safeguard the foundation of the nation. As far as our observations are concerned, we examine the trends of the times, express our thoughts, and there are things we can say.

Zhang's military rebellion and kidnapping of the commander-in-chief has already been the target of unanimous condemnation from all parties, so there is no need for us to reiterate his crimes. But just focusing on the point of soldiers harming the people, it can be concluded that he has no way to survive. Because the people are the foundation of the country, and power is intangible. It is only permissible to maintain peace and order, how can they be destroyed and massacred? When the ancient kings launched wars, they mostly said it was to comfort the people and punish the guilty. Zhou scholars wrote books and made statements, placing the people above the ruler, the country, and the altars. The insights were consistent. Since then, hegemons have emerged one after another. Considering their achievements, the first was to secure the people. Tyrants, indulging in their desires, slaughtered at will. When the people's grievances reached a boiling point, destruction followed. This is a clearly recorded historical fact that we cannot enumerate. Furthermore, in recent times, after the revolution, the national system was renewed, and the people's sentiments were greatly developed, far surpassing the past. Any actions that violated the will of the people were fraught with setbacks and failures. Yuan Shikai died because of his imperial ambitions, and Zhang Xun perished because of his restoration attempt. Coming down to the Zhili-Anhui War and the Zhang-Wu conflict, the people's support was clear. Even looking at the recent Sui incident, the nationwide enthusiastic donations were able to bolster the courage of the soldiers at the front, and ultimately the national army won successive victories, and the arrogance of the traitors was completely eliminated. Is this not enough to serve as a warning? Since the establishment of the National Government, it has promoted Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of People's Livelihood, and has earnestly sought to allow the people to rest and recuperate. On the one hand, it has worked hard to curb extortion, and on the other hand, it has tried to respect public opinion. Repeated injunctions demonstrate sincerity. Therefore, the whole country can cheer and support it unanimously, leading to today's unified situation. Now, Zhang, contrary to the government's benevolent policies, uses his personal interests to disturb the local area and indulges in harming the people. Not to mention the gathering of large armies and the disparity in strength between eggs and rocks, just speaking of this one point, it is not difficult to predict the fate of his future.

Yasukawa Succeeds as President of the South Manchuria Railway Company 38

(Tokyo) The government officially issued an order on the 21st, approving the resignation of Nagayuki Takayama as president of the South Manchuria Railway Company, and appointing Yunosuke Yasukawa as president of the South Manchuria Railway Company. (Allied Press, 21st)

(Tokyo) The new President of the South Manchuria Railway Company, Yasukawa, spoke about his aspirations on the 20th, saying, "I am entrusted with the important task of President of the South Manchuria Railway Company at an old age, and I feel the heavy responsibility. The mission of the South Manchuria Railway Company is even greater given the current state of the East Asian economy, and its future business plans must be carefully considered. Economic development must be carried out from the perspective of human coexistence and co-prosperity, and actions that unnecessarily provoke overseas sensitivities should be avoided. I will always base my actions on actions rather than words, and strive to achieve practical results. The cooperation of the whole country is especially necessary at this time." (Allied Press, 21st)

American Peace Conference; Neutrality Issue Causes Complications; Whether Neutrality Applies Outside of the Americas; Final Meeting to Achieve Results 39

Argentina, the capital. The Pan-American Peace Conference has made significant progress in promoting cooperation among the countries of North and South America. However, the United States' desire for the American continent to declare strict neutrality in the event of wars outside the continent has not been achieved. Resolutions obtained in the last 24 hours indicate that most American countries agree to approve conventions related solely to the Americas. Argentina alone views the current conference as the foundation for world peace. Although the plan for a Pan-American International League has been submitted to Washington for study, most representatives here do not agree with it. The work of the various committees has come to an end. A plenary session will be held again today, and the closing ceremony will be held on Wednesday. Matters to be discussed at today's meeting include the review of the committee's report on the "Declaration of Solidarity and Cooperation among American Countries" proposed by a certain Central American country, and several other economic proposals. (Reuters, 21st)

Argentina, the capital. The Pan-American Peace Conference recently passed three important conventions. One stipulates that the signatory countries agree not to interfere in the internal affairs of other signatory countries. The second stipulates the establishment of a collective security system. The third stipulates the joint maintenance of peace. Today, the Peace Group Organization Committee of the Peace Conference passed a motion stipulating that countries outside the Americas shall not participate in the above three conventions. However, the Argentine delegation submitted a reservation, stating that the Argentine government believes that the above three conventions should have a universal nature so that all countries in the world can participate. (Havas, 20th)

Japan-Russia Negotiations; Fisheries Treaty; Shigemitsu Visits Russian Foreign Minister 40

(Tokyo) Regarding the signing of the Japan-Soviet fisheries treaty, as a result of Ambassador Shigemitsu's meeting with Foreign Minister Litvinov on the 19th, it was decided to continue the meeting with Deputy Foreign Minister Stomonyakov on the 21st to discuss specific issues. The meeting on the 21st was actively requested by the Soviet side. It is expected that the Soviet side will actively propose some conditions, and it is believed that the outcome of this meeting will largely determine the future of the fisheries treaty signing issue. (Allied Press, 21st)

(Tokyo) Director-General Togo of the East Asia Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Chief Kase of the First Section, Chief Matsumoto of the Treaty Section, Officer Saito, Chief Ide of the Supervisory Section of the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, and related members held a meeting to discuss the Japan-Russia fisheries treaty issue. After the meeting, Director-General Togo visited Foreign Minister Arita at 6 p.m. to report on the meeting and exchange views. According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Soviet Union should be obligated to conclude a fisheries treaty in accordance with Article 11 of the Japan-Russia Peace Treaty and Article 15 of the Japan-Russia Fisheries Treaty. Therefore, if the Soviet Union cannot sign the fisheries treaty due to domestic procedures, it should find a way to extend the validity of the current treaty. Under this view, Japan believes that the Soviet Union should extend the validity of the treaty to avoid the Soviet Union's delaying tactics. (Allied Press, 21st)

On the Eve of Christmas; Pope Calls for Peace; Broadcasting to the World 41

Vatican City. The Pope will broadcast to the world on the eve of Christmas, and it is expected that he will call for peace. (Reuters, 21st)

Vatican City. Regarding the Pope Pius XI's illness, rumors circulated yesterday that it had suddenly worsened, but this is unfounded. In fact, there has been no change. He is still resting in bed according to the advice of Professor Amidei, the doctor. This morning, he also summoned Cardinal Pacelli, the Secretary of State of the Holy See. There are now plans to specially make a chair so that the Pope can sit comfortably with his right leg straight when he gets out of bed during the day. However, this plan will only be implemented when the Pope's condition definitely improves. (Havas, 21st)

Vatican City. Officials indicated today that the Pope occasionally suffers from asthma and has some difficulty breathing, but his breathing is usually very smooth, and his body temperature and pulse are no different from ordinary people. (National Telegram, 20th)

Japanese Navy Prepares to Conclude; New Pacific Treaty; Wants to Consolidate Naval Defense with Minimum Expenditure; But is also Prepared to Compete with Britain and America 42

(Tokyo) The Washington Naval Treaty will expire on January 1 next year. The Japanese Navy's budget has reached a huge sum of 680 million yen. There will be fierce discussions in the current Diet session regarding military expenses, new military plans, and shipbuilding issues. Naval authorities, including Vice-Minister Yamamoto and Director-General Toyoda of the Military Affairs Bureau, are studying how to respond in the Diet. As a result, the following decisions have been made:

(1) The purpose of the Japanese Navy's new armaments plan is to build a navy that does not threaten or invade, and to implement the minimum necessary replenishment. If the Washington and London treaties continue to exist, Japan originally planned to implement a plan to build replacement warships starting next year, so naval spending will naturally increase. The budget for the first year of the treaty's expiration is not much different from the budget when it is in effect, and in fact, the actual amount is less than when it is in effect.

(2) The Japanese Navy's replenishment plan for the post-treaty era is by no means aimed at maintaining the same number of warships as the British and American navies. It wants to build a navy that does not threaten or invade other countries, and that is most suitable for Japan's national conditions in terms of quality and type of warships, with the least expenditure. Therefore, Japan has no intention of inducing competition. However, military preparations have a comparative nature, so if Britain and America take actions that induce competition, Japan may have no choice but to compete with them.

(3) The Japanese Navy intends to compensate for any deficiencies by organizing and training fleets, in order to secure national defense. Only then will there be economic significance to military preparedness.

(4) Regarding the issue of limiting Pacific defenses, the Japanese Navy is prepared to conduct negotiations and conclude a fair treaty that adapts to the current situation in the Pacific. (Allied Press, 21st)

Ministry of Foreign Affairs of Japan Refreshes Personnel; Director-General of the East Asia Bureau to be Replaced; Morishima Succeeds Kuwashima; Other Movements as Well 43

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita, in order to refresh the personnel within the Ministry, has decided to implement a fairly wide range of personnel changes. Japanese Seiyukai; Attacks Diplomacy; Believes it is Humiliating to the Nation 44

(Tokyo) The Seiyukai decided on its policies for the 70th Diet session. On the morning of the 21st, it convened a joint conference of executives and members of the Policy Research Council at San'entei in Shiba Ward. Over sixty people, including Shimada and Hatoyama, attended. After Chairman Sunada delivered a speech, Kiyose reported on diplomacy, Kuramoto on internal affairs, Miyawaki on national defense, Kanemitsu on financial reform, Kimura on administrative organization, Tateshiro Takahashi on rural issues, Ryogoro Kato on small and medium-sized businesses and industries, and Kobayashi on social issues, from each department's special committee. After the report was unanimously approved, a general meeting of the Policy Research Council was held at the headquarters. Furthermore, Chairman Sunada stated the following in his address: "What I want to say during this deliberation is the recent diplomatic issues, including relations with China and Russia, which have suffered unprecedented humiliation in diplomatic history and are in a critical crisis. In August of this year, our party strongly urged the government to establish a national policy to adjust diplomacy as the foundation for a new administration, but so far there have been no concrete results, and instead, it has become a state of diplomacy that is humiliating to the nation. For the sake of the country, this is a matter of great concern. Japan lacks natural resources to cope with its vigorously increasing population, which is a major problem threatening the lives of the people. However, in order to understand this reality and maintain international peace, it is appropriate to seek a readjustment of world resources, and further promote the convening of international conferences, etc. I believe that this is the diplomatic policy of the Empire. In recent years, there have been strong proponents of economic alliances internationally, which have greatly sacrificed the interests of many ethnic groups in order to seek the survival of their countries, but this is using the unnatural operation of politics to oppress ethnic groups, and I am convinced that it has no sustainability. From this viewpoint, we will determine our national policy and advocate for it. In order to achieve this goal, I believe that it is necessary for the entire nation to have a great determination." (Allied Press, 21st)

The Future of the Philippines; The United States Should Actively Cooperate 45

(Washington) At the Foreign Policy Discussion Group, Popp published a survey report today, arguing that the Philippines and the United States should hold business talks as soon as possible to reduce the risk of the autonomous government failing. Mr. Popp said that the Philippine government should increase tariffs restricting American goods and conclude trade agreements with other countries. However, even after the Philippines becomes fully independent in 1946, American businesses should continue to enjoy preferential rights. The State Department has indicated that it intends to extend the period of economic adjustment in the Philippines, meaning that regardless of any changes in the political status of the Philippines, the United States still intends to exclude the Philippines when concluding most-favored-nation trade agreements with other countries. As for the opposition from all parties in the United States to withdrawing from the Philippines, it is actually due to relations with Japan. It is said that political circles in the Philippines also privately support an indefinite extension of the autonomous system. The United States may find a way to have China, Britain, France, the Netherlands, and other countries jointly guarantee the territorial integrity of the Philippines, and if it is violated, they will jointly implement sanctions. Otherwise, the United States must continue to maintain the independence of the Philippines on its own. However, the public naturally believes that since the United States has this responsibility, it should also retain some control over the internal affairs of the Philippines. If the United States' policy of isolationism progresses further, it may also completely abandon the Philippines. However, future relations with the Philippines will depend entirely on the United States' policy in the Far East. The achievements of the first year of the autonomous government show the enthusiasm of the Philippine people in supporting the government. The Philippine Constitution is well-structured, and if handled properly, it can serve as a solid foundation for democratic government. However, as it stands, it may become a rule-of-law dictatorship. As for the Philippine national defense plan, if the United States is at war with Japan, it may strengthen the United States' military strength, because the Philippine national defense is entirely a naval issue. At that time, the navies of the Philippines and the United States may restrain Japan and allow the United States to attack from the Aleutian Islands. (National Telegram, 20th)

For this reason, it was suggested last night that the Soviet government should take two measures as a warning for the future: (1) send warships to the Mediterranean to escort Soviet merchant ships; (2) ask the British and French governments to come forward to assist in curbing this kind of piracy." U.S. Secretary of War Advocates Expanding Army and Air Force, Increasing Aircraft to Over Two Thousand, Standing Army to 180,000 Personnel 50

(Washington) Secretary of War Woodring recently released an annual report requesting upgrades to both the Army and Air Force. He argued that the reserves and state guard personnel should be increased, the former to 150,000 and the latter to 210,000. He also proposed that the government should train 2,000 regular army officers and 10,000 reserve officers, and recruit 20,000 young soldiers. Furthermore, he advocated for accelerating the construction of aircraft, so that the U.S. Air Force could have 2,300 fighter planes in the shortest possible time. In 1937, 700 aircraft should be added (200 more than this year's additions). Woodring concluded by stating that this plan was only a means of self-defense and not intended for provocation. (20th Havas dispatch)

(Washington) U.S. Secretary of War Hoderin suggested that the U.S. standing army increase by 1,000 officers. After this is implemented, the total number of officers and soldiers in the U.S. standing army should be 180,000 by June 30, 1937. Mr. Hoodring declared that, given the current world situation, the United States must not neglect methods to ensure its national security. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Red Pimpernel Nearly Assassinated in Spanish Civil War 51

Gibraltar Tonight, a well-dressed Spaniard visited the Englishman Huchinson, known as the "Red Pimpernel" for saving Spanish refugees, at a major hotel here. His arrest caused shock among the crowd. According to Huchinson, speaking to a Reuters reporter, the man intended to kill him. It is said that the man will be charged with threatening fraud. While he was talking to Huchinson, a detective secretly listened in the next room. Before the Spanish Civil War, Mr. Huchinson was a lawyer in Malaga for ten years. When the Malaga authorities began arresting and killing those suspected of secretly communicating with the rebel army after the rebel planes bombed the town, Mr. Huchinson designed a plan to rescue many people from prison and transported them to Gibraltar in a small boat of eight tons, thus preserving many lives. Therefore, he gained the reputation of the modern "Red Pimpernel." (20th Reuters dispatch)

(Paris) According to dispatches from Madrid received here, the Nationalist army is currently increasing troop reinforcements to rush to the front line in Madrid. The Nationalist army plans to launch a major offensive before the New Year, but it is heard that Madrid is prepared to deal with everything. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Madrid In the past week, there have been extremely important military actions around the capital. A large-scale offensive by the Nationalist army on Madrid has long been expected by the general public and is now imminent. During the week, the Nationalist army launched repeated offensives from the village of Valdemoro in the south of the capital to the western suburbs of the capital, the Parque del Oeste, and the towns of Boadilla del Monte and Pozuelo de Alarcón in the northwest, in an attempt to cut off the road from Madrid to Irún. However, they were unsuccessful. According to the government army, the enemy launched repeated offensives at the above-mentioned locations, but were repelled, suffering heavy losses. It is estimated that in the battles in the above-mentioned locations, the Nationalist army suffered 1,500 fatalities, while the government army suffered 500 fatalities. The Nationalist army was blocked in the area from Casarrubios del Monte to Pozuelo de Alarcón west of the capital and was unable to advance. Therefore, they turned to launch a fierce offensive against Boadilla del Monte to contain the government army. The battle lasted for three days and nights without interruption. On December 15, the Nationalist army was repelled by the government army in the village of Valdemoro. On the 16th and 17th, they launched a fierce offensive against Boadilla del Monte, using artillery and aircraft to assist in the battle. However, the government army fought bravely and was unstoppable. Boadilla del Monte was originally a small village and has now been completely destroyed. The Nationalist army then launched offensives against the Parque del Oeste and the university area, but were also repelled. Currently, it is heard that the Nationalist army has obtained a large amount of supplies and is preparing to launch a major offensive on Madrid at the end of the year, launching a general offensive. According to the latest news, a large number of Nationalist troops have been concentrated in various locations near Madrid. However, according to military experts, the Nationalist army's current strength is insufficient to encircle the city of Madrid from the northwest and southeast. This can be seen from the recent movements of the Nationalist army. However, in the next few days, no matter how the enemy attacks, the government army will definitely resist regardless of all difficulties. San Salvador A nearby volcano suddenly erupted yesterday morning, and a violent earthquake occurred immediately in San Vicente and seven nearby villages. The houses in the town have all collapsed, with only the high tower of the town hall standing alone. The San Vicente volcano is located in the center of the disaster area. A new earthquake occurred in San Vicente this afternoon, causing the remaining walls and debris to collapse. The first shock occurred in the morning and was the most severe. Thousands of residents were holding services, and many people were injured and two pastors, one nun, three soldiers, and many women and children were crushed to death. The second earthquake occurred while many people were digging through the rubble, so there were many deaths. The bodies are now displayed in San Vicente Park. Hundreds of refugees have fled here today. According to newspaper reports, the number of dead and injured in the disaster area is increasing, with 150 people already dead in San Vicente alone. Guangdong Construction Department Opens New Fishing Zone: Located at the Mouth of the West River on Shangchuan Island, to Become the Premier Fishing Zone in South China 62

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangdong Construction Department, in order to develop the fishing industry, has, through the provincial government, earmarked five million yuan from rural reconstruction funds to handle the development of the fishing industry. The department is now proceeding to plan the development of the Shangchuan fishing zone and is formulating detailed plans. The fishing zone is located at the mouth of the West River, in Taishan County, west of Hengcui Island, and near Guanghai fishing zone and Yangjiang Zhapo, making it an excellent location for a fishing zone. The steps the department plans to take are to first investigate the various fishery conditions in the area, and to measure the area's topography and area, with a term of six months, with expenses of approximately twelve thousand yuan. The first phase of construction has also been decided: (1) the first section of the breakwater, (2) the first section of the fishing catch unloading wharf, (3) a weather station, (4) a fish warehouse, (5) a lighthouse, (6) a coal supply station, (7) a water supply station. In addition, an ice-making plant and cold storage will be established, requiring an expenditure of 200,000 yuan. The fishing zone will also be equipped with a fishing gear manufacturing factory, a net dyeing factory, a shipyard, a fish fertilizer factory, a canning factory, a radio station, etc., striving to become the premier fishing zone in South China. As active preparations are underway, its success is likely to be seen soon.

A Certain Party Convenes Secret Meeting at Jiabu Temple: Bao Yuexiang and Zhuo Shihai Appointed as Fake Frontline Commanders; Li Shouxin, as Fake Commander-in-Chief, Leads Bandits to Suidong; A Certain Party Dispatches a Chief Advisor to Accompany Li as a Military Supervisor 63

Zhangbei Dispatch: Since the Xi'an Incident, the remnants of bandits and puppets in Chahar, which were on the verge of collapse, have become restless again. Moreover, a certain party is watching from the sidelines, stirring up the dying embers and providing fuel, so that the flames of banditry are flaring up again. According to people from Jiabu Temple on the 18th, since the 12th of this month, military personnel from a certain party in Jiabu Temple have been shuttling between Jiabu Temple and Shangdu, negotiating with De Wang and a group of puppet bandit leaders, repeatedly deliberating on taking the opportunity to advance aggressively towards Suiyuan. Regarding military operations, a certain party convened a secret meeting in Jiabu Temple on the evening of the 16th, gathering De Wang, Bao Yueqing, Zhuo Shihai, Li Shouxin, Wang Jingxiu, and other traitors. It is vaguely heard that the main points of the resolutions are roughly as follows: (1) De Wang will remain stationed in Jiabu Temple to oversee the situation; (2) Bao Yueqing and Zhuo Shihai will be appointed as frontline commanders; (3) Li Shouxin will be appointed as the commander-in-chief of the front in Suidong (the rumor that it is Subei is incorrect), and all the puppet bandits, Mongolian and Rehe troops in front of Suidong will be under his control and dispatch; (4) a certain party will appoint another commander-in-chief to assist Li Shouxin, with the nature almost like the military supervisor dispatched by the imperial family in the autocratic era of our country; in addition, sixteen people will be dispatched to Li's staff headquarters to plan all military operations; (5) a request will be made to the highest leader of the forces at Koukou to quickly allocate airplanes and tanks to strengthen their forces, so as to launch a swift counterattack before the Xi'an Incident is resolved. On the evening of the 17th, De Wang and Li Shouxin jointly issued a large number of proclamations to the puppet generals and soldiers at the front, with absurd and outrageous wording.

As for the Rehe troops, more than 3,000 people have arrived in the vicinity of Guyuan and Gaohongyingzi in recent days and are advancing westward. Those advancing from Rehe towards Guyuan and Duolun continue to arrive in an endless stream. Two thousand troops under Zhang Haipeng arrived in Baochang on the evening of the 16th. More than 1,000 troops under Bao Yueqing, commander of the puppet 8th Division, also set off from Kangbao to the front of Shangdu early on the 17th, with Bao himself commanding in the army. One thousand Rehe troops under Wang Jingxiu, who had previously entered Zhangbei City from Duolun, had set off for the vicinity of Nanhaogian on the 16th. At the same time, four tanks were sent to that place and handed over to Zhang Wanqing to assist in the offense against Xinghe. At 8:00 PM on the evening of the 17th, Zhang Wanqing received the puppet side's general offensive order. Zhang immediately prepared to officially launch an attack from Nanhaogian towards Xinghe.

Now, it is the height of winter, and the climate outside the Great Wall is particularly cold. The fuel for the puppet bandit troops is extremely scarce. Therefore, since the army started, it has been difficult to obtain cooked hot food to ward off hunger and cold. The puppet bandits are therefore forcibly extorting from the people. Recently, merchants and residents in Kangbao and other counties are required to provide twenty catties of baked flatbreads or fried rice every day, which are continuously transported by trucks to Jiabu Temple and the front lines of Shangdu to be shared among the bandits. However, after arriving, the flatbreads are frozen, as hard as iron, and the bandits still cannot get their fill. As for the price given to the merchants and residents, each household is only given five corners, and at most no more than seven corners. The people's food is taken away, so everyone deeply hates the puppet bandits. (18th)

Fuzhou Grain and Finance: Civil Affairs Department Formulates Measures for Adjusting Grain; Provincial Government and Chamber of Commerce Plan Financial Relief 65

Fuzhou Dispatch: In recent months, due to the excessive export of rice from coastal counties in this province, although the late rice harvest was abundant, rice prices have continued to soar, which will develop into a public food panic. Various groups have repeatedly petitioned the provincial government and the civil affairs department to find ways to prohibit it. Now, the Civil Affairs Department has formulated temporary measures for adjusting grain in this province and issued them to the counties for compliance: (1) The export of rice and grain overseas is strictly prohibited. If any smuggling is discovered, it will be confiscated in full. (2) The export of rice and grain out of the province should be reported to the local county government and forwarded to the provincial government for verification and issuance of a passport before export is allowed. When it arrives at the destination, it should be reported to the local county government for verification to ensure there is no mistake, and the passport should be collected and sent to the original procurement place government for investigation and forwarded to the provincial government for record. After these regulations, rice merchants cannot transport goods as freely as they did in the past, and the amount of exports has decreased slightly. Rice from upstream creeks is also coming in steadily. If the grain in the provincial capital can be slightly accumulated, the current selling price is expected not to continue to rise, or it may be slightly reduced. Furthermore, the Fuzhou Chamber of Commerce recently sent a letter to the Shantou Chamber of Commerce, inquiring whether the rice transported from Fuzhou to that place was re-exported overseas. Yesterday, the Shantou Chamber of Commerce replied, stating that "The food supply in Chaozhou and Meizhou has always been scarce and needs external assistance to maintain. Although the late rice has been harvested, it is still a poor harvest. The people's food needs still rely on external rice adjustment. As for the rice and grain handled, they are all supplied for domestic demand and there is no re-export to foreigners," and so on.

Since the Xi'an Incident, although people in Fuzhou have been shocked, the financial situation is still stable. All kinds of banknotes are still in normal use, and prices have not increased. As for the relief of the city's financial situation during the Lunar New Year, the Chamber of Commerce previously requested the provincial government to borrow five million yuan from the Bank of China, the Central Bank, the Communications Bank, and the Agricultural Bank, with real estate as collateral, or to allow the issuance of commercial mutual assistance vouchers of not more than three million yuan for relief. The provincial government believes that the issuance of mutual assistance vouchers in the form of banknotes is related to the currency system and it is difficult to obtain approval. If it is within the scope of laws, regulations, and facts, it will do its best to help it succeed. Provincial government councilors Zhang Guowei, Fang Xueli, and Du Jundong were dispatched to discuss with Chamber of Commerce members Luo Mianhou, Hong Fasui, and Chen Peikun, and ordered the various merchant guilds to review the measures and submit them for verification. Now that the end-of-year accounting period is approaching, there are already some clues about the relief measures, and the various merchant guilds will be gathered for discussion within the next few days. (December 19th)

Since the Xi'an Incident, all circles here have been extremely indignant. Merchants Run Suzhou-Wuxi Road Automobile Service 70

The Suzhou-Wuxi Highway has been fully completed and will soon be open to traffic. It is learned that the right to operate the route between Suzhou and Guangfu has been obtained by the Su-Fu Automobile Company. As for the section between Guangfu and Wuxi, it was originally planned that the Highway Administration Office of the Jiangsu Construction Department would directly operate long-distance buses. It is heard that the method has been changed and it has been decided to be run by merchants. People from Suzhou and Wuxi, such as Liu Zhengkang and Mao Mujun, are raising funds of 200,000 yuan to organize the Suzhou-Wuxi Long-Distance Bus Company. They are currently in contact with the Jiangsu Construction Department. The idea is likely to become a reality, and traffic can be implemented in the Western New Year.

Wuxi: Yangfu Road Traffic Issues 71

The Yangfu Highway, built by the Jiangsu Construction Department, has progressed rapidly since construction began this summer. At the beginning of last month, the road surface and other projects were all completed. After the Construction Department and the Xihu Company signed a traffic agreement, the company immediately began preparations. It was originally scheduled to implement traffic within the year, but due to certain reasons, it could not be implemented. The opening has been postponed to the spring of next year. It is also learned that the Kunshan-Taicang Highway was originally handled by the Highway Administration Office of the Construction Department. Now, in order to achieve unity between Suzhou and Kunshan highways, the traffic matters of the entire Su-Zhen-Tai Highway will be organized by the Xihu Company. The Construction Department is currently negotiating with the Xihu Company.

Yuanxinglong Guanghuo Zhuang in Yangzhou Wanzijie suddenly closed down yesterday due to the commercial depression and poor turnover. Jiaxing: Second Mobilization to Collect Taxes 76

The Jiaxing County Government has dispatched officials to strictly urge the collection of the first installment of land tax for the 25th year of the Republic of China and has carried out a general mobilization to complete the collection. Currently, more than 50% of the taxes have been collected. The first installment of land tax has been fined according to regulations. Since the effect of the first general mobilization was not significant, in order to correct the arrears and achieve annual liquidation, the county government has formulated a second general mobilization inspection method. From the 21st to the 31st, it will be the period for the second mobilization. However, this mobilization will use the baojia system to check the preparations of each household. The joint offices of each district have been ordered to convene a joint meeting of township chiefs, clerks, secretaries, and cadastral officials to urge progress and dispatch personnel from the county government to attend and direct. Those who have not paid in full must voluntarily pay by the 25th at the latest. Those who fail to pay after the deadline will be strictly detained and the taxes will be recovered.

Gaoyou: Demolition Subsidies for Highway 77

There are a large number of houses in the towns and cities along the Yangqing Highway, and it is stipulated that all those within five meters must be demolished. In order to show consideration, it is stipulated that grass houses will be subsidized 5 yuan per room, and those that are not completely demolished will be subsidized 1 yuan per ridge pole. Tiled houses will be subsidized 10 yuan per room, and 2 yuan per ridge pole. Multi-story buildings will be subsidized 20 yuan per room, and 4 yuan per ridge pole. After demolition to the required width, the province will, together with the Provincial Highway Administration, fill in the demolition certificate to collect expenses.

Egg Prices Drop Dramatically 78

Eight or nine out of ten people in various districts and townships in this county rely on raising chickens and laying eggs as a sideline, with an estimated output value of 500,000 to 600,000 yuan per year. In the past two months, due to the sharp decrease in egg production in various townships and the high demand in various ports, prices have risen repeatedly, reaching 25 yuan per hundred catties, which is an unprecedented rise. Unexpectedly, due to the current situation, egg prices have dropped dramatically in recent days. On the 19th, the price fell to 17 yuan per hundred catties, a difference of 8 yuan compared to a week ago.

Newspaper Prices Soar 79

The selling price of newspapers here has suddenly soared. On the 19th, each order reached 5 yuan and 7 corners, an increase of 1 yuan and 6 corners per order compared to the previous price, and it will continue to rise. In addition, the selling price of peanuts has also soared by 4 yuan recently. On the 19th, each stone sold for 14 yuan.

In terms of the financial situation, the local area is peaceful, and the stability is as constant as before. All banks are operating as usual.

National Products Industry Discusses Next Year’s

New National Products Promotion Plan

Establish a National Products Broadcasting Station

Hold Touring Propaganda Conferences

Wang Hanqiang, Xu Yunchan, Qian Zongjian, Zhu Gengtao, and other leaders of the national products industry in Shanghai, in view of the fact that although the national products industry has gradually developed in recent years under the enthusiastic advocacy of all sectors, the import of foreign goods has still increased year by year, indicating that the people of the country still need to be made aware of the promotion of national products. The representatives of major national products factories such as Dingxin Cloth Factory, Jiuxin Enamel Factory, and Taikang Food Company, including Sun Xizu, Le Fucheng, Chen Shude, Fan Tianjin, and Xu Chengde, gathered to discuss the national products propaganda plan for next year. After exchanging opinions, they decided (1) to establish a national products broadcasting station to specifically translate the advantages and market conditions of national products in order to introduce them to the people of the country and invite leaders of the national products industry to broadcast speeches; (2) to request the government to allow the widespread installation of glass display windows in public places in major cities across the country, specifically for national products manufacturers to display various samples for people to visit, so as to increase national awareness. This kind of equipment already exists in places such as the North Railway Station in Shanghai. (3) To unite 50 national products factories as the foundation and hold national products touring propaganda conferences, specifically traveling to various places in Shanghai and other cities to expand propaganda in an attractive way, so that national products can gain the loyal trust of the people of the country. The above three principles have all been decided. In addition to the first and second items, which are still in the planning stage, the third item, the touring propaganda conference, will be held for the first time in Shanghai and is already being prepared. The location has been surveyed and determined to be the Times Vocational Middle School in Caojiadu, West Shanghai. The opening ceremony is scheduled to be held on New Year's Day next year. The propaganda materials will mainly be for daily use, and other agricultural, mineral, chemical, and aquatic products will also be collected as much as possible. National products factories wishing to participate can contact the preparatory office of the association at Room 3, 3rd Floor, Ju'e Fang, Ermalu, Shanghai. The touring propaganda outside Shanghai will first be held in Nanxiang and Kunshan, and then gradually promoted in the counties along the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway. However, it is still in preparation, so the opening date has not yet been determined.

Ineffective and Difficult to Ensure Safety

Pay Attention to Gas Masks

Many Inferior Products on the Market Are Shoddily Made by Various Merchants

People Wishing to Purchase Them Can Inquire at the Air Defense Association

Gas masks and other gas defense equipment are important tools for defending against poison gas, and civilians must have them readily available in order to deal with emergencies at any time. However, the products manufactured by general industrial factories, as well as imported products, are mostly simplified and shoddily made due to limitations in raw materials or technology. The effectiveness is low and they are of little practical use. The general public, only fearing the urgency of the need and lacking the experience to distinguish them, hastily purchase them without examining their contents, spending a large amount of money only to obtain useless equipment. The impact is not insignificant. Therefore, the Ordnance Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs has now implemented an inspection. Recalling the January 28th Incident, the manufacturers produced almost mountains of such products at that time, and the public purchased them enthusiastically. Later, after the Shanghai Air Defense Association collected and inspected them, it was discovered that these devices had no effectiveness at all. If the enemy had openly released poison gas at that time, and the public had only relied on these as the only means of defense, it would have been unthinkable. The past is a lesson. Unexpectedly, in recent days, there are even more of these inferior gas masks and equipment being produced. Not only are people wasting money, but the outflow of currency is also worrying. In view of this, the Shanghai Air Defense Association has reportedly submitted a request to the Shanghai Municipal Government to ban gas masks and various gas defense equipment that have not been inspected and stamped by the Ordnance Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs. At the same time, fearing that the public may not be fully aware of this, it has also published a notice in the newspaper to prevent the public from being deceived and increasing the danger. If anyone does not know the purchase situation, they can inquire at the association, which will be able to fully inform them and provide convenience. It is hoped that the citizens of Shanghai will pay attention to this.
